                                                                   600 1451   25
 AFCI MF33 covariance data moved into these materials where there  600 1451   26
 had been no covariance data. Covariances were estimated at LANL   600 1451   27
 based on a brief analysis of experimental data and their          600 1451   28
 agreement with the ENDF/B-VII.0 central values. An exception      600 1451   29
 is elastic scattering which serves as neutron cross section       600 1451   30
 standard from 10 eV up to 1.8 MeV, with uncertainties below 1%.   600 1451   31
                                                                   600 1451   32
                                        S.Hoblit, BNL (April 2011) 600 1451   33

                                                                   600 1451   41
 ENDF/B-VI MOD 3 Evaluation, June 1996, M.B. Chadwick and          600 1451   42
           P.G. Young (LANL)                                       600 1451   43
                                                                   600 1451   44
 Los Alamos LA150 Library, produced with FKK/GNASH/GSCAN code      600 1451   45
   in cooperation with ECN Petten.                                 600 1451   46
                                                                   600 1451   47
  This evaluation provides a complete representation of the        600 1451   48
 nuclear data needed for transport, damage, heating, radioactivity 600 1451   49
 and shielding applications over the incident neutron energy       600 1451   50
 range from 1.0E-11 to 150 MeV.  The discussion here is divided    600 1451   51
 into the region below and above 20 MeV.                           600 1451   52
                                                                   600 1451   53
 INCIDENT NEUTRON ENERGIES < 20 MeV                                600 1451   54
   Below 20 MeV the evaluation is based completely on the ENDF/B-  600 1451   55
 VI.1 (Release 1) evaluation by Fu [Fu90].  The following minor    600 1451   56
 modifications were made to the ENDF/B-VI.1 evaluation:            600 1451   57
                                                                   600 1451   58
 1.  The energy range from En = 20 MeV to 32 MeV was replaced by   600 1451   59
 the LANL evaluation (described below);                            600 1451   60
                                                                   600 1451   61
 2.  The elastic, nonelastic, and total cross sections from 19 to  600 1451   62
 20 MeV were varied to join smoothly with the higher energy        600 1451   63
 values at 20 MeV.                                                 600 1451   64
                                                                   600 1451   65
 3.  The new flag, LTT=3, is used in MF=4,MT=2 to indicate that    600 1451   66
 Legendre polynomials are used below 20 MeV and probability        600 1451   67
 tabulations at higher energies. A small discontinuity exists for  600 1451   68
 MF=4,MT=2 at 20 MeV where the two different representations join. 600 1451   69
 The higher energy evaluation utilizes a tabulation in order to    600 1451   70
 overcome the inaccuracies caused by the ENDF-6 limitation of 20   600 1451   71
 for the maximum number of Legendre coefficients.                  600 1451   72
                                                                   600 1451   73
 INCIDENT NEUTRON ENERGIES > 20 MeV (12C analysis)                 600 1451   74
   The evaluation above 20 MeV utilizes MF=6, MT=5 to represent    600 1451   75
 all reaction data.  Production cross sections and emission        600 1451   76
 spectra are given for neutrons, protons, deuterons, alpha         600 1451   77
 particles, gamma rays, and all residual nuclides produced (A>5)   600 1451   78
 in the reaction chains. To summarize, the ENDF sections with      600 1451   79
 non-zero data above En = 20 MeV are:                              600 1451   80
                                                                   600 1451   81
  MF=3 MT=  1  Total Cross Section                                 600 1451   82
       MT=  2  Elastic Scattering Cross Section                    600 1451   83
       MT=  3  Nonelastic Cross Section                            600 1451   84
       MT=  5  Sum of Binary (n,n') and (n,x) Reactions            600 1451   85
       MT=102  Radiative Capture Cross Section (Estimate Only)     600 1451   86
                                                                   600 1451   87
  MF=4 MT=  2  Elastic Angular Distributions                       600 1451   88
                                                                   600 1451   89
  MF=6 MT=  5  Production Cross Sections and Energy-Angle          600 1451   90
               Distributions for Emission Neutrons, Protons,       600 1451   91
               Deuterons, and Alphas; and Angle-Integrated         600 1451   92
               Spectra for Gamma Rays and Residual Nuclei That     600 1451   93
               Are Stable Against Particle Emission                600 1451   94
                                                                   600 1451   95
 MF=33 MT=  1  Covariance file for total cross section             600 1451   96
       MT=  2  Covariance file for elastic cross section           600 1451   97
       MT=  3  Covariance file for nonelastic cross section        600 1451   98
       MT=  5  Covariance file for composite reaction cross sect.  600 1451   99
       MT=102  Covariance file for capture cross section           600 1451  100
                                                                   600 1451  101
   The evaluation is based on nuclear model calculations that have 600 1451  102
 been benchmarked to experimental data, especially for n + C12 and 600 1451  103
 p + C12 reactions [Ch96a]. We use the GNASH code system [Yo92],   600 1451  104
 which utilizes Hauser-Feshbach statistical, preequilibrium and    600 1451  105
 direct-reaction theories. Coupled-channel and spherical optical   600 1451  106
 model calculations are used to obtain particle transmission       600 1451  107
 coefficients for the Hauser-Feshbach calculations, as well as for 600 1451  108
 the elastic neutron angular distributions.                        600 1451  109
   Cross sections and spectra for producing individual residual    600 1451  110
 nuclei are included for reactions that exceed a cross section of  600 1451  111
 approximately 1 nb at any energy.  The energy-angle-correlations  600 1451  112
 for all outgoing particles are based on Kalbach systematics       600 1451  113
 [Ka88].                                                           600 1451  114
   A model was developed to calculate the energy distributions of  600 1451  115
 all recoil nuclei in the GNASH calculations (Ch96b). The recoil   600 1451  116
 energy distributions are represented in the laboratory system in  600 1451  117
 MT=5, MF=6, and are given as isotropic in the lab system. Note    600 1451  118
 that all other data in MT=5,MF=6 are given in the center-of-mass  600 1451  119
 system. This method of representation requires a modification of  600 1451  120
 the original ENDF-6 format.                                       600 1451  121
   Preequilibrium corrections were performed in the course of the  600 1451  122
 GNASH calculations using either Feshbach, Kerman, Koonin (FKK)    600 1451  123
 theory [Ch93] or the exciton model of Kalbach [Ka77, Ka85].       600 1451  124
 Discrete level data from nuclear data sheets were matched to      600 1451  125
 continuum level densities using the formulation of Ignatyuk       600 1451  126
 [Ig75] and pairing and shell parameters from the Cook [Co67]      600 1451  127
 analysis.  Neutron and charged-particle transmission coefficients 600 1451  128
 were obtained from the optical potentials, as  discussed below.   600 1451  129
 Gamma-ray transmission coefficients were  calculated using the    600 1451  130
 Kopecky-Uhl model [Ko90].                                         600 1451  131
                                                                   600 1451  132
****************************************************************   600 1451  133
                                                                   600 1451  134
 ENDF/B-VI MOD 2 Revision, July 1991                               600 1451  135
                                                                   600 1451  136
   The only changes for MOD 2 are completion of some references,   600 1451  137
 and addition of total elastic scattering uncertainties as         600 1451  138
 recommended by the Standards Subcommittee.                        600 1451  139
   "Following concerns expressed about the seemingly small         600 1451  140
  standards uncertainties, the standards subcommitte  has provided 600 1451  141
  expanded uncertainties.  These uncertainties are estimates such  600 1451  142
  that if a modern day experiment were performed today on a given  600 1451  143
  standard using the best techniques, those results should fall    600 1451  144
  within these expanded uncertainties (2/3 of the time). They take 600 1451  145
  into account data inconsistencies and concerns about R-Matrix    600 1451  146
  parameters.  Note that it is not assumed that the uncertainties  600 1451  147
  are totally correlated within the energy ranges given. It is     600 1451  148
  recommended that these expanded uncertainties be put in file 1   600 1451  149
  and in the documentation for the standards."                     600 1451  150
 Quote from Standards Subcommittee CSEWG minutes for the May 1990  600 1451  151
 meeting.                                                          600 1451  152
                                                                   600 1451  153
 C(n,n) Total elastic scattering cross section                     600 1451  154
                                                                   600 1451  155
     Energy (keV)                 Uncertainty (%)                  600 1451  156
     1 - 500                        0.46                           600 1451  157
     500 - 1500                     0.53                           600 1451  158
     1500 - 1800                    0.60                           600 1451  159

 NEW EVALUATION FOR VERSION VI:                                    600 1451  166
 1. Total and elastic scattering from 0.1 to 0.25 MeV and from 1.6 600 1451  167
    to 1.9 MeV due to inclusion of C13 resonances [Fu88].          600 1451  168
 2. Elastic angular distribution: 0.1 to 2.0 MeV due to 13C        600 1451  169
    effects [Fu88].                                                600 1451  170
 3. New evaluation for all File 3 data 5-32 MeV by Axton [Ax88],   600 1451  171
    including new data for (n,n'3a) [An86, Br84, Me84, Ol87], for  600 1451  172
    (n,n') [Ba85, Gu81, Sa81], and for kerma factors [Be81, Br83,  600 1451  173
    Bu85, De84, De85, De86, Di82, Ha84, Mc86, We79].               600 1451  174
 4. Extention of energy and angular distributions to 32 MeV were   600 1451  175
    mostly based on extrapolation.  File 33 was extended to 32 MeV 600 1451  176
    with the addition of the new LB=8 subsubsection.               600 1451  177
                                                                   600 1451  178
   Retained from ENDF/B-V (with negligible changes such as         600 1451  179
 Q-values):  all data between 2.0 and 5.0 MeV [Fu78], all energy   600 1451  180
 and angular data for neutron and gamma-ray productions, and       600 1451  181
 uncertainty files (LB=8 subsubsection added).                     600 1451  182
                                                                   600 1451  183
   Data and evaluation techniques used in the new evaluation and   600 1451  184
 ENDF/B-V evaluation, as adopted here, are summerized below.       600 1451  185

 MF-MT                                                             600 1451  187
 3-1 TOTAL                                                         600 1451  188
    1.E-5 eV TO 4.81 MeV -- sum of 3-2 and 3-102.                  600 1451  189
    4.81 MeV TO 20 MeV -- [Sc67, Ci69, Pe72].                      600 1451  190
 3-2 ELASTIC SCATTERING                                            600 1451  191
    1.E-5 eV to 4.81 MeV --  R-Matrix analysis with data [Sc67,    600 1451  192
      Ci69, Pe72, Ah70, Bl75, Di68, Fr70, He75, La57, La61, La69,  600 1451  193
      Me70, Ki76, Ho72, Ho75, St70, Me54, Wi58, Kn73, Pu64, El62,  600 1451  194
      We65, Ke65, Go65, Ga72, Pk72]. Bayes theorem (or nonlinear   600 1451  195
      least square) used for energies less then 2 MeV, resulting   600 1451  196
      weights were then used in the R-Matrix analysis.  A thermal  600 1451  197
      total cross section of 4.746 +- 0.025 (evaluated by Lubitz   600 1451  198
      [Lu76]) was also used in the R-Matrix fit.                   600 1451  199
    4.81 MeV to 8 MeV -- [Ga72, Ve73, Pk72].                       600 1451  200
    8 MeV to 14 MeV -- [Ha75, Ve73, Pu76].                         600 1451  201
    14 MeV to 32 MeV -- [Bo68, Me84].                              600 1451  202
    R-Matrix analysis for C13 below 2 MeV with data of [La81,      600 1451  203
     He75, Co61, Au79].                                            600 1451  204
